            <li className="flex items-start gap-2">
              <span className="text-terracotta mt-0.5">⚠️</span>
              <span><strong>Important:</strong> Stay on this page until upload completes!</span>
            </li>
          </ul>
        </div>

        {/* Video Grid */}
        {data.videos.length > 0 && (
          <div>
            <h3 className="text-lg font-semibold text-charcoal mb-4">
              Uploaded Videos ({data.videos.length})
            </h3>
            <div className="grid grid-cols-1 md:grid-cols-2 gap-6 mb-6">
              {data.videos.map((video) => (
                <div
                  key={video.id}
                  className="relative p-4 bg-white border-2 border-sand/40 rounded-xl group hover:border-sage/40 transition-all"
                >
                  {/* Video Player */}
                  <div className="relative aspect-video rounded-lg overflow-hidden bg-charcoal/10 mb-3">
                    <video
                      controls
                      preload="metadata"
                      className="w-full h-full object-cover"
                      poster={video.thumbnail}
                    >
                      <source src={video.url} type="video/mp4" />
                      Your browser does not support the video tag.
                    </video>
                  </div>

                  {/* Video Title */}
                  <input
                    type="text"
                    value={video.title}
                    onChange={(e) => updateVideoTitle(video.id, e.target.value)}
                    placeholder="Video title..."
                    className="w-full px-3 py-2 border border-sand/40 rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-sage/30 text-sm font-medium mb-2"
                  />

                  {/* File Info */}
                  <div className="flex items-center justify-between text-xs text-charcoal/60">
                    <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                      <Film size={12} /> Video
                    </span>
                    {video.duration && (
                      <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
                        <Play size={12} />
                        {video.duration}
                      </span>
                    )}
                  </div>

                  {/* Remove Button */}
                  <button
                    onClick={() => removeVideo(video.id)}
                    className="absolute top-2 right-2 p-2 bg-charcoal/80 hover:bg-charcoal rounded-full transition-all opacity-100 lg:opacity-0 lg:group-hover:opacity-100 shadow-lg"
                    title="Remove video"
                  >
                    <Trash2 size={14} className="text-ivory" />
                  </button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>
        )}

        {/* Upload Area */}
        <div
          onClick={() => !uploading && data.videos.length < 10 && videoRef.current?.click()}
          data-tutorial="videos"
          className={`border-2 border-dashed rounded-xl p-16 text-center transition-all ${uploading
              ? 'opacity-70 cursor-wait'
              : data.videos.length >= 10
                ? 'border-sand/20 cursor-not-allowed opacity-50'
                : 'border-sand/40 cursor-pointer hover:border-sage/40 hover:bg-sage/5'
            }`}
        >
          {uploading ? (
            <div className="flex flex-col items-center justify-center">
              <div className="w-12 h-12 border-4 border-sage/30 border-t-sage rounded-full animate-spin mb-4" />
              <p className="text-sage font-medium text-lg">{uploadProgress}</p>
              <p className="text-charcoal/60 text-sm mt-2">⚠️ Please stay on this page until upload completes</p>
            </div>
          ) : data.videos.length >= 10 ? (
            <>
              <div className="mb-6 relative inline-block">
                <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-sand/20 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                  <Film size={48} className="text-charcoal/30" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-charcoal/40 mb-2">
                Maximum Videos Reached
              </h3>
              <p className="text-charcoal/40 mb-6 max-w-md mx-auto">
                You have uploaded the maximum of 10 videos for this archive.
              </p>
            </>
          ) : (
            <>
              <div className="mb-6 relative inline-block">
                <div className="w-24 h-24 bg-gradient-to-br from-terracotta/20 to-sage/20 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center">
                  <Film size={48} className="text-charcoal/40" />
                </div>
              </div>
              <h3 className="text-xl font-semibold text-charcoal mb-2">
                {data.videos.length === 0 ? "Upload Your First Video" : "Add More Videos"}
              </h3>
              <p className="text-charcoal/60 mb-6 max-w-md mx-auto">
                Click here to upload video files. You can select multiple videos at once.
              </p>
              <div className="inline-flex items-center gap-2 px-6 py-3 bg-sage hover:bg-sage/90 text-ivory rounded-xl font-medium transition-all">
                <Upload size={20} />
                Choose Video Files
              </div>
            </>
          )}
        </div>

        <input
          ref={videoRef}
          type="file"
          accept="video/*"
          multiple
          onChange={handleVideoUpload}
          className="hidden"
          disabled={uploading}
        />
      </div>

      {/* Navigation */}
      <div className="mt-12 flex gap-4">
        <button
          onClick={onBack}
          disabled={uploading}
          className="px-6 py-4 border border-sand/40 rounded-xl hover:bg-sand/10 transition-all font-medium disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          ← Back
        </button>
        <button
          onClick={onNext}
          disabled={uploading}
          className="flex-1 bg-terracotta hover:bg-terracotta/90 text-ivory py-4 px-6 rounded-xl font-medium transition-all disabled:opacity-50"
        >
          {data.videos.length > 0 ? 'Save & Continue to Review →' : 'Skip Videos & Continue →'}
        </button>
      </div>

      {/* Tutorial Popup */}
      {showTutorial && (
        <TutorialPopup
          steps={tutorialSteps}
          onComplete={handleTutorialComplete}
          onSkip={handleTutorialSkip}
        />
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

===== FICHIER: ./content/legal/content-policy.md =====

# Content Policy & Community Standards

**Last Updated:** February 2, 2026

⚠️ **IMPORTANT NOTICE**: This document includes temporary DMCA procedures (Section 6) that provide good-faith copyright protection until Legacy Vault registers a designated DMCA agent with the U.S. Copyright Office. For immediate copyright concerns, contact copyright@legacyvault.com.

---

## 1. Our Commitment

Legacy Vault is a sacred space for memorialization. This policy ensures we maintain dignity, protect families, and comply with legal obligations while balancing the deeply personal nature of remembrance.

**By creating a memorial, you agree to:**
- Only upload content you own or have permission to use
- Respect the privacy and dignity of the deceased and their families
- Indemnify Legacy Vault against disputes arising from your memorial content
- Accept our Family Dispute Resolution procedures

---

## 2. Prohibited Content (Zero Tolerance)

The following will result in immediate removal and potential account termination:

### 2.1 Copyright Violations
- **Professional photos**: Photographer portraits, stock images, news photos you don't own
- **Music**: Songs in tribute videos without proper licensing
- **Text**: Copied obituaries, articles, or book excerpts without permission
- **Artwork**: Paintings, drawings, or designs you didn't create

**Temporary Process**: Copyright holders should email copyright@legacyvault.com with proof of ownership. We remove infringing content within 48 hours of verification. Repeat infringers will be banned.

### 2.2 Graphic and Disturbing Content
- Death imagery (bodies, autopsy photos, crime scenes)
- Graphic violence or medical trauma images
- Content intended to shock or traumatize

**Exception**: Peaceful open-casket photos with content warnings are permitted if culturally appropriate.

### 2.3 Sexual Content
- Nudity, pornography, or sexual acts
- Revenge porn (intimate images shared without consent)
- Sexualization of the deceased

### 2.4 Defamation and False Claims
- Knowingly false statements harming the deceased's reputation
- False accusations (crimes, abuse) without legal documentation
- Fabricated quotes or achievements

### 2.5 Privacy Violations
- Medical records or private diagnoses without authorization
- Financial information, addresses, phone numbers of living family
- Private messages or hacked/leaked communications
- Photos of minors without parental consent

### 2.6 Hate and Harassment
- Hate speech targeting race, religion, gender, orientation, or disability
- Content created to mock or ridicule the deceased
- Harassment of surviving family members through the memorial

### 2.7 Illegal Content
- CSAM (Child Sexual Abuse Material) — reported to law enforcement immediately
- Evidence of crimes or instructions for illegal acts
- Fraud, scams, or phishing attempts

---

## 3. Family Dispute Resolution (Critical)

### 3.1 The "Family War Zone" Protocol
Families often disagree about memorial content. We do not take sides. Our only goal is legal compliance and platform safety.

**Examples of disputes we see:**
- Second wife vs. adult children from first marriage
- Siblings arguing over "unflattering" photos
- Estate executor claiming memorial creator had no authority
- Ex-spouses disputing representation of marriage

### 3.2 Our Neutral Stance
**Legacy Vault does not:**
- Judge family conflicts or determine "truth"
- Mediate estate disputes
- Determine who "deserves" to control the narrative
- Provide legal advice

**Legacy Vault does:**
- Follow legal documentation (court orders, estate papers)
- Provide a 30-day dispute resolution process
- Remove content that violates this policy or law
- Protect ourselves from liability through your Memorial Authorization Form

### 3.3 Dispute Resolution Process

**Step 1: Informal Resolution (Days 1-7)**
We encourage families to resolve issues privately. Contact the memorial creator directly if possible.

**Step 2: Formal Complaint (Days 8-14)**
Email disputes@legacyvault.com with:
- Your relationship to deceased
- Specific content in dispute (URLs, screenshots)
- Legal basis (privacy rights, defamation, copyright)
- Evidence supporting your claim
- What resolution you seek (removal, editing, transfer of control)

**Step 3: Temporary Action (Days 15-21)**
- We may temporarily hide disputed content pending resolution
- Memorial creator is notified and given 7 days to respond
- If memorial creator provides legal authority (probate documents, authorization), content may be restored
- If no legal documentation provided, content remains hidden

**Step 4: Final Resolution (Days 22-30)**
- **Content stays**: If memorial creator demonstrates legal authority and content doesn't violate policy
- **Content removed**: If violation confirmed, no legal authority shown, or court order received
- **Court order required**: For complex disputes we cannot adjudicate, we require court documentation

### 3.4 Authority Hierarchy
When disputes arise, we give weight to (in order):
1. **Court orders or legal injunctions**
2. **Estate executor with probate documentation**
3. **Spouse (if legally married at death)**
4. **Adult children (majority consensus)**
5. **Parents of deceased**
6. **Memorial Authorization Form submitted at creation**

*Note: Without legal documentation, we default to the memorial creator who submitted the Authorization Form.*

### 3.5 No Liability for Family Conflicts
**You explicitly agree**: Legacy Vault is not liable for:
- Emotional distress from family disputes
- Removal or retention of disputed content
- Legal costs incurred by any party
- Damages arising from family disagreements

**Protection**: Your Memorial Authorization Form requires you to indemnify us against claims from other family members.

---

## 4. Post-Mortem Privacy and Dignity

### 4.1 Respect for the Deceased
- No mockery, satire, or ridicule
- No exploitation contrary to the person's known wishes
- No disclosure of private information the deceased kept confidential in life

### 4.2 Public Figures vs. Private Individuals
**Private individuals** receive higher privacy protections. **Public figures** allow broader historical discussion, but still subject to prohibitions on defamation and graphic content.

### 4.3 Cultural Sensitivity
We respect diverse mourning traditions. Content should not gratuitously violate cultural or religious norms regarding the dead.

---

## 5. Temporary DMCA Copyright Procedure

⚠️ **TEMPORARY PROCEDURE**: Legacy Vault has not yet registered a designated DMCA agent with the U.S. Copyright Office. The following good-faith procedure provides copyright protection until formal registration is completed.

### 5.1 Reporting Copyright Infringement
If you believe your copyrighted work is on our platform without authorization:

**Email**: copyright@legacyvault.com

**Include**:
1. Your name and contact information
2. Description of the copyrighted work (photo, music, text, etc.)
3. Exact URL where the infringing material appears
4. Statement that you have a good faith belief the use is not authorized
5. Statement that the information is accurate, under penalty of perjury
6. Your electronic or physical signature

### 5.2 Our Response
- **Review**: We assess claim within 48 hours
- **Removal**: If claim appears valid, we remove or disable access to the material
- **Notification**: We notify the user who posted the content
- **Record**: We keep records of takedowns for repeat infringer policy

### 5.3 Counter-Notification (If Your Content Was Removed)
If you believe your content was removed by mistake:

**Email**: copyright@legacyvault.com with subject "Counter-Notification"

**Include**:
1. Your name and contact information
2. Description of removed content and where it appeared
3. Statement under penalty of perjury that you have a good faith belief the material was removed by mistake
4. Statement that you consent to jurisdiction of federal court in Delaware
5. Your electronic or physical signature

**Restoration**: If we receive a valid counter-notification, we may restore the content after 10 business days unless we receive notice that a lawsuit has been filed.

### 5.4 Limitations
**This temporary procedure**:
- Does not provide full DMCA safe harbor protection
- Is a good-faith effort to respect copyright rights
- Will be replaced with formal DMCA procedures upon registration of a designated agent
- Does not constitute legal advice

**For copyright holders**: If you require formal DMCA compliance immediately, please contact us to arrange expedited processing or legal coordination.

### 5.5 Repeat Infringers
Users with multiple valid copyright complaints will have their accounts terminated and memorials removed.

---

## 6. Reporting Violations

### 6.1 How to Report
**Email**: reports@legacyvault.com

**Include**:
- URL of memorial
- Description of violation (which policy section)
- Your relationship to content (family, rights holder, visitor)
- Evidence or explanation
- Your contact information

### 6.2 Review Process
- **Initial review**: 48 hours
- **Investigation**: We examine content against policy and context
- **Action**: Removal, warning, suspension, or no action
- **Notification**: Reporter and content owner notified (unless safety concern)

### 6.3 Appeals
**Email**: appeals@legacyvault.com within 14 days
- Explain why the decision was incorrect
- Provide additional context
- Senior team reviews within 7 days (decision is final)

---

## 7. Consequences

### 7.1 Warning System
- **First violation**: Warning and content removal
- **Second violation**: 7-day suspension
- **Third violation**: Permanent termination

### 7.2 Immediate Termination
Accounts will be immediately terminated for:
- CSAM (reported to law enforcement)
- Terrorism/extremist content
- Severe harassment or threats
- Fraud or impersonation

### 7.3 No Refunds
Accounts terminated for policy violations forfeit refunds per our Refund Policy.

---

## 8. Changes to This Policy

We may update this policy to address new issues or legal requirements. Material changes will be notified 30 days in advance. Continued use constitutes acceptance.

**Next Planned Update**: Registration of formal DMCA agent and expansion of dispute resolution procedures.

---

## 9. Contact

- **General Reports**: reports@legacyvault.com
- **Copyright**: copyright@legacyvault.com  
- **Family Disputes**: disputes@legacyvault.com
- **Appeals**: appeals@legacyvault.com

**Address**:  
Legacy Vault LLC  
Attn: Content Policy Department  
123 Main Street  
Wilmington, DE 19801

---

**By creating a memorial on Legacy Vault, you affirm that you have read, understood, and agree to abide by this Content Policy, including the requirement to indemnify Legacy Vault against family disputes and copyright claims.**
===== FICHIER: ./content/legal/memorial-authorization.md =====

# Memorial Authorization Form

**Version 1.0** | **Effective Date:** February 2, 2026  
**Required for all memorial creations on Legacy Vault**

---

## ⚠️ CRITICAL LEGAL NOTICE

**READ CAREFULLY BEFORE SIGNING:** This is a legally binding document. By signing below, you enter into a contractual agreement with Legacy Vault LLC that includes indemnification clauses, representations of legal authority, and waivers of liability. If you do not understand these terms, consult an attorney before proceeding.

**Purpose:** This form establishes your legal authority to create a memorial for a deceased person and protects Legacy Vault from claims by other family members, estates, or third parties.

---

## Section 1: Memorial Creator Information

### 1.1 Your Identity (Required)
I, the undersigned, represent and warrant that the following information is true and accurate:

**Full Legal Name:** _________________________________________________  
**Date of Birth:** _________________________________________________  
**Current Address:** _________________________________________________  
**City, State, ZIP:** _________________________________________________  
**Email Address:** _________________________________________________  
**Phone Number:** _________________________________________________  

### 1.2 Relationship to Deceased (Check all that apply)
- [ ] Spouse (legally married at time of death)
- [ ] Domestic Partner (registered or recognized)
- [ ] Adult Child (age 18 or older)
- [ ] Parent
- [ ] Sibling
- [ ] Grandchild
- [ ] Estate Executor (court-appointed)
- [ ] Estate Administrator (court-appointed)
- [ ] Attorney representing Estate
- [ ] Other: ______________________ (specify relationship)

### 1.3 Authority Verification
I represent and warrant that I am:
- [ ] The legally authorized representative of the deceased's estate
- [ ] The next of kin with legal authority to make memorial decisions
- [ ] Acting with the consent of all persons with superior post-mortem rights
- [ ] Authorized by court order to create this memorial

**If Estate Representative:** Attach copy of Letters Testamentary or Letters of Administration (required)

---

## Section 2: Deceased Person Information

### 2.1 Identity of Memorial Subject
**Full Legal Name of Deceased:** _________________________________________________  
**Date of Birth:** _________________________________________________  
**Date of Death:** _________________________________________________  
**Place of Death:** _________________________________________________  
**Last Known Residence:** _________________________________________________  

### 2.2 Estate Information
**Has probate been opened?**  
- [ ] Yes (Probate Case Number: ______________________ Jurisdiction: ______________________)  
- [ ] No (Estate is small/affidavit procedure)  
- [ ] Unknown  
- [ ] Not applicable (no estate assets)

**Name of Estate Executor/Administrator:** _________________________________________________  
**Executor Contact Information:** _________________________________________________  

---

## Section 3: Legal Authority Representations

### 3.1 Authority to Create Memorial
I represent and warrant that:

**A. I have the legal right** to create this memorial and make decisions regarding the deceased's post-mortem representation, including:
- Selecting photographs and visual representations
- Writing or approving biographical content
- Determining privacy settings (public vs. private)
- Inviting other family members to contribute
- Making editorial decisions about the narrative

**B. I have obtained consent** from (check applicable):
- [ ] The estate executor/administrator
- [ ] The surviving spouse
- [ ] All adult children
- [ ] The deceased's parents (if no spouse/children)
- [ ] Other persons with post-mortem rights: ______________________
- [ ] I am the sole person with post-mortem rights (explain): ______________________

**C. No conflicting claims:** To my knowledge, no other person:
- Has claimed exclusive authority over the deceased's memorialization
- Has objected to my creation of this memorial
- Has threatened legal action regarding this memorial

### 3.2 Post-Mortem Rights Acknowledgment
I understand that:
- **Post-mortem privacy rights** exist in many jurisdictions and may be held by the estate or family members
- **Right of publicity** may survive death in certain states (California, Indiana, Nevada, etc.)
- **Defamation of the dead** may be actionable in some jurisdictions
- **Cultural/religious rights** may apply to certain types of memorialization

I represent that I have considered these rights and have authority to proceed.

---

## Section 4: Content Representations

### 4.1 Accuracy of Information
I represent and warrant that:
- All biographical information I provide is **true and accurate** to the best of my knowledge
- I will not knowingly include **false or defamatory** statements about the deceased
- I will not include **unsubstantiated allegations** of criminal conduct, abuse, or other harmful acts without legal documentation
- I have the right to use all **photographs, videos, and media** I upload

### 4.2 Copyright and Intellectual Property
I represent and warrant that:
- I own or have obtained licenses for all content I upload
- I understand that **professional photographer portraits** are typically owned by the photographer, not the subject
- I will not upload **copyrighted music, text, or images** without permission
- I grant Legacy Vault a license to host and display the content I upload

### 4.3 Privacy and Consent
I represent and warrant that:
- I have obtained consent from **living persons** depicted in photos or mentioned in stories (or they are public figures)
- I will not disclose **private medical information** without authorization
- I will not share **financial information, addresses, or phone numbers** of living family members
- I will respect the **privacy wishes** the deceased expressed during their lifetime

---

## Section 5: Indemnification and Hold Harmless

### 5.1 Indemnification Agreement
**THIS IS A BINDING INDEMNIFICATION CLAUSE. READ CAREFULLY.**

I agree to **indemnify, defend, and hold harmless** Legacy Vault LLC, its officers, directors, employees, agents, successors, and assigns (collectively, "Legacy Vault") from and against any and all claims, demands, actions, suits, proceedings, damages, liabilities, losses, costs, and expenses (including reasonable attorneys' fees) arising out of or relating to:

**A. Family Disputes:** Any claim by family members, heirs, or other interested parties disputing:
- My authority to create this memorial
- The content or portrayal of the deceased
- Editorial decisions or omissions
- Inclusion/exclusion of certain family members or information

**B. Legal Violations:** Any claim that the memorial violates:
- Post-mortem privacy rights
- Right of publicity
- Copyright or intellectual property laws

- False or misleading

### 5.2 Scope of Protection

- Reimburse Legacy Vault for legal costs within 30 days of invoice

# Privacy Policy

**Last Updated:** February 2, 2026

---

## 1. Introduction: A Sacred Trust

At Legacy Vault, we understand that we are not merely storing data—we are safeguarding the most precious memories of your life and the lives of those you love. This Privacy Policy explains how we collect, use, store, and protect your information in accordance with the highest standards of digital stewardship.

We treat your memorial data with the same care and reverence that you would give to a family archive. Our commitment to privacy is inseparable from our commitment to durability: just as we promise to preserve your memories for generations, we promise to protect them with equal dedication.

---

## 2. Information We Collect

### 2.1 Account Information
When you create a Legacy Vault account, we collect:
- **Identity**: Your name and email address
- **Authentication**: Encrypted password (hashed using bcrypt)
- **Payment Data**: Billing information processed securely through Stripe (we never store full credit card numbers on our servers)
- **Preferences**: Your communication preferences and account settings

### 2.2 Memorial Content
The heart of our service involves preserving rich biographical content:
- **Biographical Data**: Names, dates, places, life stories, career histories, family relationships
- **Media**: Photographs, videos, audio recordings, documents, and scanned materials
- **User Contributions**: Stories, memories, and tributes added by you or invited family members
- **Metadata**: Upload dates, file sizes, geolocation data (if included in uploaded files), and organizational tags

### 2.3 Usage Information
To improve our service and ensure security, we collect:
- **Technical Data**: IP addresses, browser type, device information, operating system
- **Activity Logs**: Access times, pages viewed, features used, and memorial viewing statistics
- **Cookies**: Essential session cookies and optional analytics cookies (see Section 9)

### 2.4 Concierge Service Data
For our Concierge tier ($6,500 white-glove service), we additionally collect:
- **Consultation Notes**: Information shared during Zoom calls or email correspondence
- **Processing Metadata**: Notes on how materials are organized and presented
- **Temporary Working Files**: High-resolution copies during the digitization and editing process

---

## 3. How We Use Your Information

### 3.1 Service Provision
We use your data to:
- Create, host, and display your memorial pages
- Process and optimize uploaded media (resizing images for web display, transcoding videos)
- Enable family collaboration through invitation systems
- Provide customer support and technical assistance
- Process payments and maintain billing records

### 3.2 Concierge Service Delivery
For Concierge clients specifically:
- **Human Review**: Our trained staff accesses your uploaded materials to craft your memorial narrative
- **Communication**: Coordinating via email, Zoom, or phone to understand your vision
- **Quality Assurance**: Internal review of completed memorials before publication
- **Secure Handling**: All Concierge staff sign confidentiality agreements and undergo privacy training

### 3.3 Legal and Security
- **Compliance**: Meeting tax obligations, responding to legal requests, enforcing our Terms of Service
- **Protection**: Detecting fraud, preventing abuse, and ensuring platform security
- **Rights Management**: Verifying your authority to create memorials for deceased persons through our Memorial Authorization process

### 3.4 Service Improvement
- **Analytics**: Using anonymized usage data to improve user experience (we use privacy-focused analytics that do not track individuals across sites)
- **Feedback**: Incorporating user suggestions and troubleshooting issues

---

## 4. Data Sharing and Disclosure

### 4.1 Your Control Over Visibility
- **Private Memorials**: Only you and invited collaborators can view content
- **Public Memorials**: Visible to anyone with the link or found through search (you control this setting)
- **Collaborative Access**: When you invite family members via email, they gain access to contribute content to specific memorials

### 4.2 Service Providers
We share data only with trusted third parties necessary to operate our service:

| Provider | Purpose | Data Shared |
|----------|---------|-------------|
| **Supabase** | Database hosting and storage | All memorial content, account data |
| **Stripe** | Payment processing | Billing information, transaction history |
| **Zoom** | Concierge consultations (if chosen) | Video call metadata, recordings (if consented) |
| **Vercel** | Website hosting | Technical logs, IP addresses |

All providers are contractually obligated to use your data solely for providing their services to us and are GDPR-compliant where applicable.

### 4.3 Legal Requirements
We may disclose information:
- **Court Orders**: In response to valid legal process, subpoenas, or court orders
- **Protection**: When necessary to protect our rights, property, or safety, or that of our users
- **Fraud Prevention**: To investigate violations of our Terms or fraudulent payment activity

### 4.4 Business Transfers
If Legacy Vault is acquired, merges with another entity, or sells assets, your data will transfer to the new owner subject to the same privacy commitments. We will notify you via email 30 days before any such transfer.

### 4.5 What We Never Do
**We do not sell, rent, or trade your personal information or memorial content to third parties for marketing purposes.** We do not use your memorial photos in advertising. We do not train AI models on your private content.

---

## 5. Data Retention and Deletion

### 5.1 Active Accounts
Your data remains stored as long as your account is active. We maintain:
- **Primary Storage**: Live databases with real-time access
- **Backups**: Encrypted backups retained for 90 days to enable recovery from technical failures
- **Archives**: Long-term archival storage for durability promises

### 5.2 Account Deletion
When you delete your account:
- **Grace Period**: 30 days to reverse deletion if changed your mind
- **Permanent Deletion**: After 30 days, all personal identifiers and memorial content are permanently erased from active databases
- **Backup Expiration**: Encrypted backups containing your data expire naturally within 90 days
- **Legal Retention**: Payment records retained for 7 years per tax regulations (stripped of memorial content)

### 5.3 Concierge Project Retention
For completed Concierge projects:
- **Working Files**: Temporary high-res copies and draft materials deleted 30 days after memorial publication
- **Final Deliverables**: Preserved indefinitely per your durability plan unless you delete your account
- **Communication Records**: Email threads and consultation notes retained for 2 years for quality assurance

---

## 6. Your Rights and Choices

Depending on your location, you have specific rights regarding your personal data:

### 6.1 For All Users (Global)
- **Access**: Request a complete copy of your data at any time
- **Correction**: Edit or update any information in your memorials
- **Export**: Download your entire memorial as a ZIP file containing HTML, JSON, and all media (guaranteed portability)
- **Deletion**: Close your account and permanently delete your data

### 6.2 GDPR Rights (EU/UK Users)
If you are in the European Union or United Kingdom:
- **Right to be Forgotten**: Request immediate erasure of personal data
- **Data Portability**: Receive your data in a structured, machine-readable format
- **Restriction**: Request we limit processing while disputes are resolved
- **Objection**: Object to processing based on legitimate interests
- **Consent Withdrawal**: Revoke permission for specific processing activities

### 6.3 CCPA Rights (California Residents)
If you are a California resident:
- **Know**: Request disclosure of categories and specific pieces of personal information collected
- **Delete**: Request deletion of personal information (with certain exceptions)
- **Opt-Out**: Direct us not to sell your personal information (though we never sell data, we honor this request formally)
- **Non-Discrimination**: We will not discriminate against you for exercising privacy rights

### 6.4 Deceased Persons' Rights
We recognize that memorials often contain information about deceased individuals. While privacy laws vary by jurisdiction regarding post-mortem rights:
- **Estate Authority**: Estates or authorized representatives may request modification or removal of memorials
- **Family Disputes**: We maintain a neutral stance and may require legal documentation to resolve conflicts between family members
- **Dignity**: We reserve the right to remove content that defames the deceased or causes undue harm to surviving family members

### 6.5 How to Exercise Rights
Submit requests to: **privacy@legacyvault.com**

Response time: 30 days (may extend to 60 days for complex requests). We will verify your identity before processing sensitive requests.

---

## 7. Security Measures

### 7.1 Technical Safeguards
- **Encryption**: AES-256 encryption for data at rest; TLS 1.3 for data in transit
- **Access Control**: Role-based access controls; staff access logged and audited
- **Infrastructure**: SOC 2 Type II certified hosting through Supabase
- **Monitoring**: 24/7 security monitoring for unauthorized access attempts

### 7.2 Concierge Security Protocols
For our white-glove service:
- **Confidentiality Agreements**: All Concierge staff sign NDAs and privacy pledges
- **Device Security**: Staff work on encrypted, company-managed devices only
- **Access Limits**: Staff can only access projects assigned to them; no broad database access
- **Audit Trails**: Every access to your memorial data is logged with timestamp and action

### 7.3 Incident Response
In the unlikely event of a data breach:
- **Notification**: We will notify affected users within 72 hours of discovery
- **Transparency**: Clear communication about what data was involved and steps taken
- **Mitigation**: Immediate action to secure systems and prevent recurrence
- **Support**: Credit monitoring or identity protection services offered if sensitive financial data is involved

---

## 8. International Data Transfers

Legacy Vault is based in the United States. Your data is stored on servers located in the United States (US East region).

### 8.1 For EU/UK Users
We transfer data from the EU/UK to the US using:
- **Standard Contractual Clauses (SCCs)**: EU Commission-approved contractual safeguards
- **Data Processing Agreements**: Legally binding contracts with our processors ensuring GDPR-equivalent protection

### 8.2 Your Rights Regarding Transfers
You may request information about the specific safeguards in place for international transfers by contacting our Data Protection Officer.

---

## 9. Cookies and Tracking Technologies

### 9.1 Essential Cookies
Required for basic functionality:
- **Session Management**: Authentication tokens to keep you logged in
- **Security**: CSRF protection tokens
- **Preferences**: Language and accessibility settings

### 9.2 Analytics Cookies
We use privacy-respecting analytics (Plausible or Fathom) that:
- Do not use cookies by default
- Do not track you across the internet
- Do not collect personal identifiers
- Provide anonymized traffic patterns only

### 9.3 Third-Party Cookies
Our payment processor (Stripe) may set cookies necessary for fraud prevention and payment security. These are governed by Stripe's privacy policy.

### 9.4 Managing Cookies
You can disable cookies in your browser settings, though this may affect functionality. Our cookie banner allows granular control for EU visitors.

---

## 10. Children's Privacy (COPPA Compliance)

### 10.1 Age Requirements
Legacy Vault is intended for users **18 years of age or older**. We do not knowingly collect personal information from children under 18.

### 10.2 Memorials of Minors
If creating a memorial for a deceased child:
- **Parental Consent**: Must be created by a parent or legal guardian
- **Enhanced Privacy**: These memorials default to private and require explicit consent for any public sharing
- **Sensitive Handling**: We treat child memorials with additional care and expedited support for family disputes

If you believe we have inadvertently collected information from a child under 18 without parental consent, contact us immediately at **privacy@legacyvault.com** for immediate deletion.

---

## 11. Changes to This Privacy Policy

We may update this policy to reflect changes in our practices or legal requirements.

- **Material Changes**: For significant changes (new data uses, new sharing practices), we will email you 30 days in advance
- **Minor Updates**: For clarifications or non-substantive changes, we will update the "Last Updated" date at the top of this page
- **Archive**: Previous versions available upon request

Your continued use of Legacy Vault after changes constitutes acceptance of the updated policy.

---

## 12. Contact Information

### Data Protection Officer
For privacy-specific inquiries, GDPR requests, or data protection concerns:

**Email:** privacy@legacyvault.com

Legacy Vault LLC  
Attn: Data Protection Officer  
123 Main Street  
Wilmington, DE 19801  
United States

### Response Times
- **Standard Requests**: 30 days
- **Urgent Security Issues**: 72 hours
- **Data Breach Notifications**: Immediate (within 72 hours of discovery)

---

## 13. Special Provisions for Concierge Service

Given the intimate nature of our $6,500 Concierge tier, we provide additional privacy guarantees:

### 13.1 Human Handling Protocols
- **Staff Vetting**: All Concierge staff undergo background checks
- **Privacy Training**: Annual training on handling sensitive family materials
- **Project Isolation**: Your materials are accessible only to your assigned Concierge team

### 13.2 Communication Privacy
- **Zoom Calls**: Recorded only with explicit consent; recordings encrypted and deleted after project completion
- **Email**: Communications retained for 2 years then purged
- **Voice Messages**: Transcribed for accessibility; originals deleted after memorial publication

### 13.3 Post-Project Cleanup
After your Concierge memorial is finalized:
- Draft materials and working copies deleted within 30 days
- Only final, approved content retained in your permanent archive
- All temporary access tokens revoked

---

**By using Legacy Vault, you entrust us with your most precious memories. We honor that trust through rigorous privacy protection, transparent practices, and unwavering commitment to your family's dignity.**

# Refund & Cancellation Policy

**Last Updated:** February 2, 2026

**Effective Date:** February 2, 2026

---

## 1. Overview

Legacy Vault creates permanent digital memorials that require significant preparation, storage allocation, and curation work. Due to the nature of digital memorialization services and the immediate costs we incur upon purchase (server provisioning, support team allocation, curation preparation), we maintain a structured refund policy that balances fairness to our customers with protection against abuse.

**By purchasing a Legacy Vault memorial, you acknowledge and agree to this Refund & Cancellation Policy.**

---

## 2. General Principles

### 2.1 Service Nature
Our memorials are **custom digital services** that include:
- Permanent cloud storage allocation
- Professional curation and formatting (Family Plan)
- Immediate server resource provisioning
- Support team assignment
- Domain/URL reservation

Once work begins or digital assets are delivered, the service is considered partially or fully consumed.

### 2.2 Cooling-Off Period
We offer a **30-day cooling-off period** for cancellations before memorial publication. After publication, the memorial is considered complete and delivered, making it ineligible for refund except in specific circumstances outlined below.

### 2.3 Family Dispute Exception
We recognize that memorialization can trigger family conflicts. We provide a **Family Dispute Refund** pathway that supersedes standard policy when valid legal documentation is provided.

---

## 3. Personal Plan Refunds ($300)

### 3.1 Before Publication (Draft Status)
- **Full refund** available within 30 days of purchase if memorial has not been published
- **Cancellation**: You may cancel anytime before publication for full refund
- **Processing time**: 5-7 business days to original payment method

### 3.2 After Publication (Live Status)
- **No refunds** once memorial is published and live
- **Reason**: Digital product delivered, storage allocated, URL active
- **Transfer option**: You may transfer ownership to another family member instead of cancellation

### 3.3 Partial Work Exception
If you request significant customization beyond standard templates before publication:
- **Over 2 hours of custom work**: 50% refund only (remaining 50% covers labor costs)
- **Under 2 hours of custom work**: Full refund under 3.1

---

## 4. Family Plan Refunds ($3,000)

### 4.1 Before Curation Begins
- **Full refund** available if curation team has not started work
- **Status check**: Email refunds@legacyvault.com to confirm work status
- **Timeline**: Typically 5 business days after purchase if no work started

### 4.2 During Curation (Work in Progress)
- **50% refund** if curation has begun but memorial not yet published
- **Calculation**: Covers labor costs already incurred by curation team
- **Cancellation**: Memorial will not be completed or published

### 4.3 After Publication
- **No refunds** once Family Plan memorial is published
- **Deliverables**: Includes professional curation, custom design, family tree setup, permanent hosting
- **Service complete**: Work is considered fully delivered upon publication

### 4.4 Multi-Payment/Installment Plans
If you selected installment payments:
- **Cancellation before completion**: Cease future payments, no refund of prior payments if work has begun
- **Cancellation before work starts**: Full refund of payments made
- **Default**: If you stop paying installments, memorial remains in draft status until paid in full or cancelled per 4.1

---

## 5. Family Dispute Exception (All Plans)

### 5.1 Eligibility
If a family dispute arises regarding the memorial with **valid legal documentation**:

**Qualifying documentation**:
- Court order regarding estate authority
- Cease and desist letter from licensed attorney representing estate
- Documentation proving memorial creator lacked legal authority
- Evidence of fraudulent purchase (identity theft, unauthorized card use)

### 5.2 Refund Terms
- **Full refund** issued to original purchaser
- **Memorial removal**: Complete deletion of all content
- **No penalties**: Family dispute refunds do not count against refund limits
- **Timeline**: Processed within 10 business days of documentation verification

### 5.3 Process
1. Email disputes@legacyvault.com with documentation
2. Our team verifies legal validity (may require attorney consultation)
3. If valid, refund issued and memorial removed within 72 hours
4. If insufficient documentation, standard refund policy applies

### 5.4 No Documentation Refunds
Without legal documentation, family disagreements do **not** qualify for exception refunds. You must use our Content Policy dispute resolution process instead.

---

## 6. Cancellation Process

### 6.1 How to Cancel
Email **refunds@legacyvault.com** with:
- Account email address
- Memorial URL or name
- Reason for cancellation
- Confirmation you understand refund terms

### 6.2 Timeline
- **Response**: Within 2 business days
- **Refund processing**: 5-10 business days after approval
- **Method**: Original payment method (credit card, bank account)

### 6.3 What Happens After Cancellation
- **Before publication**: All data deleted, URL released, no trace remains
- **After publication**: Not applicable (no cancellations accepted)
- **Family Plan mid-work**: Draft content deleted, curation stops

### 6.4 Reactivation
Cancelled memorials can be reactivated within 30 days by repurchasing at original price. After 30 days, data is permanently purged and cannot be recovered.

---

## 7. Non-Refundable Circumstances

### 7.1 No Refunds For:
- **Policy violations**: Accounts terminated for Content Policy violations (hate speech, copyright, illegal content)
- **Change of mind**: After publication, "I don't want it anymore" is not grounds for refund
- **Technical issues on user end**: Browser compatibility, user device problems
- **Failure to use**: Not logging in or not adding content
- **Price changes**: If prices drop after your purchase

### 7.2 Chargebacks Prohibited
**You agree not to initiate chargebacks** with your credit card company or bank without first contacting us and allowing 10 business days to resolve the issue.

**Chargeback consequences**:
- Account immediate termination
- Memorial removal
- Collection proceedings for chargeback fees ($25-100 per dispute)
- Ban from future service

**If you have a legitimate dispute**: Contact refunds@legacyvault.com first. We resolve 95% of issues without chargebacks.

---

## 8. Subscription Billing (If Applicable)

If Legacy Vault introduces recurring subscription elements:
- **Monthly/Annual plans**: Cancel anytime, prorated refund for unused days
- **Auto-renewal**: Charged automatically unless cancelled 24 hours before renewal
- **Cancellation**: Via account settings or email to refunds@legacyvault.com

*Currently, Legacy Vault operates on one-time purchases only.*

---

## 9. Special Circumstances

### 9.1 Death of Purchaser
If the person who purchased the memorial dies before publication:
- **Estate may request**: Full refund to estate or transfer to family member
- **Documentation**: Death certificate and proof of estate authority required
- **Timeframe**: Must request within 1 year of death

### 9.2 Technical Failure on Our End
If Legacy Vault experiences catastrophic technical failure preventing memorial publication:
- **Your choice**: Full refund OR wait for resolution + service credit
- **Definition**: Server outage >30 days, data loss on our end (not user error)
- **Force Majeure**: Natural disasters, acts of war, internet infrastructure failure do not qualify

### 9.3 Fraudulent Purchases
If you did not authorize the purchase (identity theft, stolen card):
- **Immediate refund** upon verification
- **Cooperation required**: You must file police report and provide case number
- **Account security**: We will help secure the account

---

## 10. Currency and Payment Methods

### 10.1 Currency
All prices and refunds are in **USD (United States Dollars)**. 

**International customers**: Refund amounts may vary slightly due to:
- Currency exchange rate fluctuations
- International transaction fees (non-refundable)
- Bank conversion fees

### 10.2 Payment Methods
- **Credit/Debit Cards**: Refunded to same card (5-10 business days)
- **Bank Transfer**: Refunded to same account (7-14 business days)
- **Digital Wallets** (Apple Pay, Google Pay): Refunded to wallet (3-5 business days)

---

## 11. Dispute Resolution

### 11.1 Good Faith Requirement
You agree to attempt resolution with us directly before:
- Initiating chargebacks
- Filing small claims lawsuits
- Posting public complaints
- Regulatory complaints

### 11.2 Our Commitment
We commit to:
- Respond to all refund requests within 2 business days
- Provide clear explanation if refund denied
- Offer alternatives (credits, transfers) where appropriate
- Treat each request with empathy given the memorial context

### 11.3 Escalation
If you disagree with our refund decision:
- **Appeal**: Request senior review within 14 days
- **Mediation**: We agree to non-binding mediation in Delaware (costs split)
- **Small Claims**: You may file in Delaware small claims court (if under $10,000)

---

## 12. Changes to This Policy

We may update this policy with 30 days notice for material changes. Current policy at time of purchase governs your transaction.

**Grandfathering**: If you purchased under a previous policy, that policy applies to your refund eligibility.

---

## 13. Contact Information

**Refund Requests**: refunds@legacyvault.com  
**Family Disputes**: disputes@legacyvault.com  
**Billing Issues**: billing@legacyvault.com  
**General Questions**: support@legacyvault.com

**Response Times**:
- Refund requests: 2 business days
- Dispute documentation: 5 business days
- Appeals: 7 business days

**Mailing Address**:  
Legacy Vault LLC

TERMS OF SERVICE

**Last Updated:** [DATE_TO_BE_UPDATED]

---

## 1. ACCEPTANCE OF TERMS

By accessing or using Legacy Vault (the "Service"), you agree to be bound by these Terms of Service ("Terms"). If you do not agree to these Terms, do not use the Service.

These Terms constitute a legally binding agreement between you and Legacy Vault LLC ("Legacy Vault," "we," "us," or "our").

**You must be at least 18 years old to use this Service.** By using the Service, you represent that you are at least 18 years of age and have the legal capacity to enter into this agreement.

---

## 2. SERVICE DESCRIPTION

### 2.1 What Legacy Vault Is

Legacy Vault is a digital memorial and archive creation service that allows users to create, organize, and preserve biographical information, photographs, videos, documents, and other content related to themselves or deceased persons.

### 2.2 What Legacy Vault Is NOT

Legacy Vault is NOT a funeral home, funeral service provider, or estate planning service. We do not provide legal advice, mediate family disputes, or determine the accuracy of biographical information.

### 2.3 Service Tiers

Legacy Vault offers three service tiers:

- **Personal Archive** ($1,500): Individual memorial creation for one person
- **Family Archive** ($3,000): Multiple memorials within a family structure with cross-linking capabilities
- **Concierge Archive** ($6,500): Full-service memorial creation with professional assistance (subject to separate Concierge Service Agreement)

## 4. USER ELIGIBILITY & AUTHORITY

### 4.1 Legal Authority

**CRITICAL:** By using the Service to create a memorial for a deceased person, you represent and warrant that:

- You have the legal authority to create such memorial
- You are next of kin, executor of the estate, legal representative, or have obtained proper consent
- You have informed relevant family members of your intent to create the memorial
- To your knowledge, no family member or legal representative objects to the creation of the memorial
- You have the right to upload and share all content you provide

### 4.2 Memorial Authorization Form

Before creating a memorial for a deceased person, you must complete and submit our Memorial Authorization Form, which constitutes a separate binding agreement.

### 4.3 Compliance with Laws

You agree to comply with all applicable local, state, national, and international laws and regulations in your use of the Service.

You retain all ownership rights to the content you upload to the Service, including:

### 6.2 License You Grant to Us

By uploading content to the Service, you grant Legacy Vault a **non-exclusive, worldwide, royalty-free license** to:
- Store your content on our servers and backup systems
- Display your content within the memorial you create
- Process your content for technical purposes (resize images, compress videos, format text)
- Create redundant copies for backup and durability purposes
- Make your content available to individuals you designate as recipients
- Perform any technical operations necessary to provide the Service

**This license continues for as long as your memorial remains active and terminates when you close your account**, except for:
- Content retained in backups (deleted within 90 days)
- Content we are required to retain by law

### 6.3 Your Warranties Regarding Content

You represent and warrant that:
- You own all content you upload OR have obtained all necessary permissions, licenses, and consents
- Your content does not infringe any third-party intellectual property rights
- Your content does not violate any person's privacy, publicity, or other personal rights
- Your content does not contain defamatory, libelous, or unlawful material
- All biographical information is accurate to the best of your knowledge

### 6.4 Copyright Infringement

If you believe any content on our Service infringes your copyright, please contact us at legal@legacyvault.com with:
- Identification of the copyrighted work
- Identification of the infringing material
- Your contact information

We reserve the right to remove allegedly infringing content and terminate accounts of repeat infringers.

### 6.5 Your Indemnification

**You agree to indemnify, defend, and hold harmless Legacy Vault** from any claims, damages, losses, liabilities, and expenses (including reasonable attorney fees) arising from:
- Content you upload that infringes third-party rights

**This means you will pay our legal costs if we are sued because of content you uploaded or representations you made.**

## 7. MEMORIAL CONTENT & PRIVACY

### 7.1 Privacy Settings

You control who can view your memorial through privacy settings. Options may include:
- Private (only you can view)
- Family & Friends (designated individuals only)
- Public (viewable by anyone with the link)

### 7.2 Memorial Sharing

You may invite others to view your memorial by:
- Sending direct invitations via email
- Sharing a private link
- Making the memorial public

You are responsible for managing access to your memorial.

### 7.3 Durability Promise

We strive to make your memorial durable and long-lasting through:
- Redundant storage systems
- Regular backups
- Decentralized technologies where appropriate
- Export capabilities

However, we cannot guarantee perpetual availability. See Section 11 (Warranty Disclaimers) for important limitations.

### 7.4 Content Policy

All content must comply with our Content & Acceptable Use Policy, which is incorporated into these Terms by reference. Prohibited content includes but is not limited to:
- Hate speech or discriminatory content
- Explicit sexual content
- Graphic violence
- Content that violates third-party rights
- Illegal content

Violation of our Content Policy may result in content removal or account termination without refund.

---

## 9. EXPORT & DATA PORTABILITY

### 9.1 Export Rights

You have the right to export your memorial data at any time. This is a core feature of our durability promise.

### 9.2 Export Format

Exports include:
- A ZIP file containing all uploaded media (photos, videos, documents)
- An HTML website that can be viewed offline
- Structured data in JSON format
- A printable biography and timeline
- A manifest file for reference

### 9.3 How to Request Export

You can request an export by:
- Using the "Export Memorial" feature in your account settings
- Contacting support@legacyvault.com
- We will provide the export within 5 business days

### 9.4 Independence from Legacy Vault

Exported memorials are designed to be **viewable and usable without Legacy Vault's Service**. This ensures your content remains accessible even if our Service becomes unavailable.

## 10. SERVICE TERMINATION

### 10.1 Termination by You

You may close your account at any time by:
- Using account closure feature in settings
- Contacting support@legacyvault.com

We recommend exporting your memorial before closing your account.

### 10.2 Termination by Legacy Vault

We may suspend or terminate your account if:
- You breach these Terms
- You upload illegal or prohibited content
- You fail to complete payment
- Your account has been inactive for more than 5 years (with 60 days' notice)
- We are required to do so by law

### 10.3 Notice Period

We will provide at least 30 days' notice before terminating your account, except in cases of:
- Illegal activity
- Severe Terms violations
- Emergency situations requiring immediate action

### 10.4 Effect of Termination

Upon termination:
- Your access to the Service will be revoked
- Your memorial will be removed from public view
- You will have 30 days to export your data
- After 30 days, your data will be permanently deleted
- Data may persist in backups for up to 90 days
- Refunds are subject to our Refund Policy

## 14. DISPUTE RESOLUTION

### 14.1 Informal Resolution First

Before initiating any formal dispute resolution, you agree to contact us at legal@legacyvault.com to attempt to resolve the dispute informally. We commit to working in good faith to resolve disputes within 30 days.

### 14.2 Binding Arbitration

**IF INFORMAL RESOLUTION FAILS, YOU AGREE THAT ANY DISPUTE ARISING FROM OR RELATING TO THESE TERMS OR THE SERVICE WILL BE RESOLVED BY BINDING ARBITRATION, NOT IN COURT.**

**Arbitration Details:**
- **Service:** American Arbitration Association (AAA)
- **Rules:** AAA's Consumer Arbitration Rules
- **Location:** Wilmington, Delaware or your location if more convenient
- **Format:** Individual arbitration only (no class arbitration)
- **Language:** English
- **Decision:** Arbitrator's decision is final and binding
- **Costs:** Each party pays their own attorney fees; arbitration fees according to AAA rules

### 14.3 Class Action Waiver

**YOU AGREE THAT DISPUTES WILL BE RESOLVED ON AN INDIVIDUAL BASIS ONLY. YOU WAIVE ANY RIGHT TO PARTICIPATE IN A CLASS ACTION, CLASS ARBITRATION, OR REPRESENTATIVE ACTION.**

### 14.4 Exceptions to Arbitration

The following disputes are NOT subject to arbitration:
- Claims in small claims court (if eligible)
- Claims seeking injunctive relief for intellectual property violations
- Claims that cannot be arbitrated under applicable law

### 14.5 Opt-Out Right

**You have 30 days from first accepting these Terms to opt out of arbitration.** To opt out, send written notice to legal@legacyvault.com stating your name, address, and clear intent to opt out of arbitration. If you opt out, disputes will be resolved in court.

### 14.6 Survival

This arbitration provision survives termination of these Terms.
